 pakistan kaa sabase bada or vyast jinna international airport

 At exactly 11:30 pm, five terrorists enter inside the Old Terminal Building near Pakistan International Airlines
 paanchon pakistani airport kii suraksha ke jimmedaar aesuef yani airport security force kii vardi main the
 All the terrorists were in ASF uniform
 
 
 in paanchon ke daakhil hone ke kuch hi second ke andar paanch or aatankwaadi uske baraabar vaale duusare get se old terminal main ghus jate hai

 The Suri founder Suri ruled northern India from 1540 to 1556
 2
 Issued rupee for the first time in the reign 3
 Suri reconstructed the city of Pataliputra and named it Patna
 4
 Sher Shah was also known for hunting tigers

 Extended the Grant Truck Road from Chittagong, which now exists from Bangladesh to Kabul

 He died in an explosion in the fort of Kalingar while fighting a war against the Chandel Rajputs

 1
 ausat masik balance (average Monthly Balance yaa AMB) kam ho jane par lagaaya jane vaala jurmaana : bhartiya state bank ne aaj, yani 1 oktober se apni shahari, ardhshahri tathaa gramin shakhaon ke graahakon, yani khataadharakon ke liye ausat masik balance kii seemaa ko gata diya he

 Charges for transfer through National Electronic Funds Transfer or NEFT or Real Time Gross Settlement: Transactions through NEFT and RTGS through digital medium Will remain, but a fee will be charged for such a transaction by going to the branches of the bank
 10,000 rupee tak ke NEFT transaction par graahak ko 2 rupee tathaa GST chukaana hoga
 On NEFT transactions ranging from Rs 10,000 to Rs 1,00,000, Rs 4 and GST will have to be paid

 On RTGS transactions ranging from Rs 2,00,000 to Rs 5,00,000, the customer will have to pay Rs 20 and GST, while RTGS transactions of over Rs 5,00,000 will pay Rs 40 and GST
 3
 Cash Deposit and Withdrawal: Any customer can make three transactions free of cost for depositing cash in the savings accounts of State Bank of India, but after that the account holder will be charged Rs 50 and GST for each transaction
 jis shakha main khaataa nahin he, usamen nakadi jamaa kii adhiktam seemaa 2,00,000 rupee pratidin hogi
